Non Stop Blackjack 21 fun is here!\r\nBlackjack is also know as 21 or twenty-one is a widely played casino banking game. \r\n\r\nBlackjack 21 is a comparing card game between a player and a dealer, meaning players will compete against a dealer but not against other players and is played with one or more decks of 52 cards. \r\n\r\nA Blackjack 21 game can be won in the following ways:\r\n\r\n✔ Getting 21 points on the player's first 2 cards which is called a 'blackjack', 'natural' assuming the dealer has not got a blackjack\r\n✔ Get a score higher than the dealer without exceeding 21\r\n✔ Allowing the dealer to draw additional cards until his hand exceeds 21\r\n\r\nWhen the game of blackjack 21 starts the player or players are dealt with a two card hand and add together the value of their cards. The Face cards which are kings, queens and jacks are counted as 10 points. The dealer and the player count an ace as 1 point or 11 points, and all other cards are counted according to the numeric value shown on the card. The players after receiving their first two cards, have an option of getting a hit or taking an additional card. When a player uses their boost, the worm loses some mass, causing the worm's size to shrink slightly, with the mass that is lost from the boost appearing as a line of small pellets where the boost was used. The mass lost can be regained by consuming the pellets. Similar to pellets dropped from defeated avatars, the boost pellets correspond to the color of the avatar. The boost feature is useful to outmaneuver and defeat opponents.[4] A common strategy that is used by players to defeat opponents is of the player's avatar coiling around the opponent's in a loop, until the opponent, trapped in the loop, crashes into the player.\r\n\r\nThere is a border that confines avatars within the circular game board. If a worm hits the border, the player automatically dies without turning into the aforementioned pellets. As of now it is removed, in 2016, the player with the biggest worm at the end of the day was able to share a \"victory message\" with the world.
